### [140] [FireBridge: Cycle-Accurate Hardware + Firmware Co-Verification for Modern Accelerators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25969)
*G Abarajithan,Zhenghua Ma,Francesco Restuccia,Ryan Kastner*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: FIREBRIDGE 提供了一种快速且循环准确的硬件-固件联合验证框架，通过使用标准模拟器并编译固件为 x86，实现了从固件调试、性能分析到验证的全流程加速，同时保持功能等效。与基于 FPGA 的传统流程相比，FIREBRIDGE 在不同类型的加速器上将调试迭代速度提高了最多 50 倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着加速器的复杂性增加，硬件和固件集成成为生产力瓶颈，尤其是对于依赖 FPGA 仿真进行硬件与固件集成的开发人员来说，调试迭代和时间上市都被显著延迟。因此，需要一种能够加速硬件和固件联合验证的方法，特别是在现代加速器验证中至关重要的功能包含测试、数据移动分析和内存拥塞模拟。

Method: FIREBRIDGE 利用标准模拟器（如 VCS、Vivado Xsim 或 Xcelium）并通过编译固件为 x86 来简化支持，并通过随机化的内存桥将模拟子系统连接起来。这种方法允许对硬件和固件进行全面和循环准确的联合验证，并促进了多功能测试、数据移动分析和寄存器级协议检查等功能。

Result: FIREBRIDGE 实现了对于不同类型的加速器（如阵列处理器和 CGRAs）在 RTL/HLS 和生产固件之间的系统集成，相较于传统的基于 FPGA 的流程，加速了调试迭代，最多可实现 50 倍的提速，确保了功能等效性和广泛的适用性。

Conclusion: FIREBRIDGE 通过提供一种快速且循环准确的硬件-固件联合验证框架，加速了异构计算平台的开发流程，提升了系统的集成效率，并支持团队进行有组织和并行的开发工作。

Abstract: Hardware-firmware integration is becoming a productivity bottleneck due to the increasing complexity of accelerators, characterized by intricate memory hierarchies and firmware-intensive execution. While numerous verification techniques focus on early-stage, approximate modeling of such systems to speed up initial development, developers still rely heavily on FPGA emulation to integrate firmware with RTL/HLS hardware, resulting in significant delays in debug iterations and time-to-market. We present a fast, cycle-accurate co-verification framework that bridges production firmware and RTL/gate-level hardware. FIREBRIDGE enables firmware debugging, profiling, and verification in seconds using standard simulators such as VCS, Vivado Xsim, or Xcelium, by compiling the firmware for x86 and bridging it with simulated subsystems via randomized memory bridges. Our approach provides off-chip data movement profiling, memory congestion emulation, and register-level protocol testing, which are critical for modern accelerator verification. We demonstrate a speedup of up to 50x in debug iteration over the conventional FPGA-based flow for system integration between RTL/HLS and production firmware on various types of accelerators, such as systolic arrays and CGRAs, while ensuring functional equivalence. FIREBRIDGE accelerates system integration by supporting robust co-verification of hardware and firmware, and promotes a structured, parallel development workflow tailored for teams building heterogeneous computing platforms.

</details>


### [141] [IBEX: Internal Bandwidth-Efficient Compression Architecture for Scalable CXL Memory Expansion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26131)
*Younghoon Ko,Hyemin Park,Hyuk-Jae Lee,Hyokeun Lee*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 文章提出了一种名为IBEX的块级压缩方案，通过仅压缩冷数据、优化内部带宽管理和采用影子促进方案来提高性能，从而在不牺牲速度的情况下增加了内存容量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的内存扩展器受到物理限制，难以实现可扩展的内存容量扩展，因此需要新的压缩方案来提升内存效率。

Method: IBEX方案采用了基于推进的方法，仅对冷数据进行压缩，同时优化了块管理以减少元数据访问开销，并提出了影子推进方案以缓解决除分配带来的性能影响。

Result: IBEX在相比现有基于推进的块级压缩方法中获得了1.28x-1.40x的平均性能提升。

Conclusion: IBEX通过对冷数据进行压缩优化以及优化块管理和提出影子推进方案，成功实现了内存容量的扩大和性能的提升。

Abstract: As the memory channel count is confined by physical dimensions, memory expanders appear to be a promising approach to extending memory capacity and channels by augmenting the existing I/O interface (e.g., PCIe) with memory-semantic protocols like CXL. Unfortunately, the physical constraints of a computing system restrict scalable capacity expansion with memory expanders. In this work, we propose a block-level compression scheme for modern memory expanders, IBEX, to achieve larger effective memory capacity. Given the performance overhead associated with block-level compression algorithms (e.g., LZ77), IBEX employs a promotion-based approach: only cold data is compressed, whereas hot data remains uncompressed. Our key innovation is internal bandwidth-efficient block management that precisely identifies cold pages with minimal metadata access overhead. Still, the promotion-based approach poses several performance-related challenges at the design level. Therefore, we also propose a shadowed promotion scheme that temporarily postpones the deallocation of promoted data, thereby mitigating the performance penalty incurred by demotion (i.e., recompression). Furthermore, we optimize our compression scheme by compacting metadata and co-locating multiple target blocks for efficient bandwidth utilization. Consequently, IBEX achieves an average of 1.28x-1.40x speedups compared to the state-of-the-art promotion-based block-level approaches. We open-source IBEX at https://github.com/relacslab/ibex-ics26.

</details>
